(s *Server) boolean(ctx context.Context, flag *flipt.Flag, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BooleanEvaluationResponse, error) {\n\trollouts, err := float32(int(hash) % 100)\n\n\t\t\t// if this case does not hold, fall through to the next rollout.\n\t\t\tif normalizedValue < rollout.Threshold.Percentage {\n\t\t\t\tresp.Enabled =
